2765:                            <script>
2766:                                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
2767:                                    const estimatedShipping = document.querySelector('#esimated-shippingtemplate--26212660740439__main2edbf491-d07c-4718-b71e-18ffe22ab7dc');
2768:                                    if (estimatedShipping) {
2769:
2770:                                        const months = estimatedShipping.getAttribute('data-month-labels').split(',');
2771:                                        const days = rearrangeDays(estimatedShipping.getAttribute('data-day-labels').split(','));
2772:
2773:                                        const originalText = estimatedShipping.getAttribute('data-text');
2774:                                        const shippingMinDays = parseInt(estimatedShipping.getAttribute('data-min-days'));
2775:                                        const shippingMaxDays = parseInt(estimatedShipping.getAttribute('data-max-days'));
2776:                                        const dateFormat = estimatedShipping.getAttribute('data-date-format');
2777:                                        const textContainer = estimatedShipping.querySelector('.estimated-shipping__text');
2778:
2779:                                        const currentDate = new Date();
2780:
2781:                                        const startDate = addDays(currentDate, shippingMinDays);
2782:                                        var startDateDaySuffix = 'th';
2783:                                        const startDay = startDate.getDate();
2784:                                        if (startDay === 1 || startDay === 21 || startDay === 31) startDateDaySuffix = 'st';
2785:                                        else if (startDay === 2 || startDay === 22) startDateDaySuffix = 'nd';
2786:                                        else if (startDay === 3 || startDay === 23) startDateDaySuffix = 'rd';
2787:
2788:                                        const endDate = addDays(currentDate, shippingMaxDays);
2789:                                        var endDateDaySuffix = 'th';
2790:                                        const endDay = endDate.getDate();
2791:                                        if (endDay === 1 || endDay === 21 || endDay === 31) endDateDaySuffix = 'st';
2792:                                        else if (endDay === 2 || endDay === 22) endDateDaySuffix = 'nd';
2793:                                        else if (endDay === 3 || endDay === 23) endDateDaySuffix = 'rd';
2794:
2795:                                        let startDateString, endDateString;
2796:                                        if (dateFormat === 'day_dd_mm') {
2797:                                            console.log('day_dd_mm')
2798:                                            startDateString = days[startDate.getDay()] + ', ' + startDate.getDate() + '. ' + months[startDate.getMonth()];
2799:                                            endDateString = days[endDate.getDay()] + ', ' + endDate.getDate() + '. ' + months[endDate.getMonth()];
2800:                                        } else if (dateFormat === 'mm_dd') {
2801:                                            console.log('mm_dd')
2802:                                            startDateString = months[startDate.getMonth()] + ' ' + startDate.getDate() + startDateDaySuffix;
2803:                                            endDateString = months[endDate.getMonth()] + ' ' + endDate.getDate() + endDateDaySuffix;
2804:                                        } else if (dateFormat === 'dd_mm') {
2805:                                            console.log('dd_mm')
2806:                                            startDateString = startDate.getDate() + '. ' + months[startDate.getMonth()];
2807:                                            endDateString = endDate.getDate() + '. ' + months[endDate.getMonth()];
2808:                                        } else if (dateFormat === 'day_dd_mm_numeric') {
2809:                                            console.log('day_dd_mm_numeric')
2810:                                            const startDateDay = String(startDate.getDate()).length > 1 ? startDate.getDate() : '0' + startDate.getDate();
2811:                                            const startDateMonth = String((startDate.getMonth() + 1)).length > 1 ? (startDate.getMonth() + 1) : '0' + (startDate.getMonth() + 1);
2812:                                            startDateString = days[startDate.getDay()] + ', ' + startDateDay + '. ' + startDateMonth + '.';
2813:
2814:                                            const endDateDay = String(endDate.getDate()).length > 1 ? endDate.getDate() : '0' + endDate.getDate();
2815:                                            const endDateMonth = String((endDate.getMonth() + 1)).length > 1 ? (endDate.getMonth() + 1) : '0' + (endDate.getMonth() + 1);
2816:                                            endDateString = days[endDate.getDay()] + ', ' + endDateDay + '. ' + endDateMonth + '.';
2817:                                        } else if (dateFormat === 'dd_mm_numeric') {
2818:                                            console.log('dd_mm_numeric')
2819:                                            const startDateDay = String(startDate.getDate()).length > 1 ? startDate.getDate() : '0' + startDate.getDate();
2820:                                            const startDateMonth = String((startDate.getMonth() + 1)).length > 1 ? (startDate.getMonth() + 1) : '0' + (startDate.getMonth() + 1);
2821:                                            startDateString = startDateDay + '. ' + startDateMonth + '.';
2822:
2823:                                            const endDateDay = String(endDate.getDate()).length > 1 ? endDate.getDate() : '0' + endDate.getDate();
2824:                                            const endDateMonth = String((endDate.getMonth() + 1)).length > 1 ? (endDate.getMonth() + 1) : '0' + (endDate.getMonth() + 1);
2825:                                            endDateString = endDateDay + '. ' + endDateMonth + '.';
2826:                                        } else {
2827:                                            // day_mm_dd
2828:                                            startDateString = days[startDate.getDay()] + ', ' + months[startDate.getMonth()] + ' ' + startDate.getDate() + startDateDaySuffix;
2829:                                            endDateString = days[endDate.getDay()] + ', ' + months[endDate.getMonth()] + ' ' + endDate.getDate() + endDateDaySuffix;
2830:                                        }
2831:
2832:                                        const textWithStartDate = originalText.replace('[start_date]', startDateString);
2833:                                        const finalText = textWithStartDate.replace('[end_date]', endDateString)
2834:                                        textContainer.innerHTML = finalText;
2835:                                    }
2836:
2837:                                    function addDays(date, days) {
2838:                                        var result = new Date(date);
2839:                                        result.setDate(result.getDate() + days);
2840:                                        return result;
2841:                                    }
2842:
2843:                                    function rearrangeDays(arr) {
2844:                                        arr.unshift(arr[6]);
2845:                                        arr.length = 7;
2846:                                        return arr;
2847:                                    }
2848:                                })
